Ryan X. Charles [Today at 10:44 PM]
re: the above idea about a Bitcoin News website to help with stuff. i will thread the idea here.
11 replies

Ryan X. Charles [5 minutes ago]
i had the idea to make a Bitcoin News some time ago - just like Hacker News, except for Bitcoin

Ryan X. Charles [5 minutes ago]
now that we have bit OP_RETURNs, we can put the entire thing on the blockchain

Ryan X. Charles [4 minutes ago]
the messages themselves can just be JSON and/or markdown

Ryan X. Charles [4 minutes ago]
we need a naming system, which i have figured out and will post shortly

Ryan X. Charles [4 minutes ago]
posts can be links or content, just like Hacker News

Ryan X. Charles [4 minutes ago]
comments are threaded

Ryan X. Charles [4 minutes ago]
next to each post is a tipping button

Ryan X. Charles [3 minutes ago]
i think that's basically it, except that moderation is a problem

Ryan X. Charles [3 minutes ago]
my idea is to charge for content

Ryan X. Charles [3 minutes ago]
that part is not decentralized - i don't have a better idea for moderation. ideas appreciated.

Ryan X. Charles [2 minutes ago]
'charge for content' just means charge to post. unless you pay Bitcoin News, your news doesn't show up on the website.
